\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a439e60a72eadecfeda2df5449c613a64}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!abs@{abs}}
\index{abs@{abs}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{abs()}{abs()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a439e60a72eadecfeda2df5449c613a64} 
template$<$typename gen\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a08b807947b47031d3a511f03f89645ad}{GLM\+\_\+\+CONSTEXPR}} gen\+Type \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga439e60a72eadecfeda2df5449c613a64}{glm::\+abs}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns x if x \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}= 0; otherwise, it returns -\/x.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em gen\+Type} & floating-\/point or signed integer; scalar or vector types.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_addf5ef73283c171730e0bcc11833fa81}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!frexp@{frexp}}
\index{frexp@{frexp}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{frexp()}{frexp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_addf5ef73283c171730e0bcc11833fa81} 
template$<$typename gen\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} gen\+Type \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gaddf5ef73283c171730e0bcc11833fa81}{glm::\+frexp}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type}]{x}{, }\item[{int \&}]{exp}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Splits x into a floating-\/point significand in the range \+[0.\+5, 1.\+0) and an integral exponent of two, such that:\+ x = significand \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} exp(2, exponent)

The significand is returned by the function and the exponent is returned in the parameter exp. For a floating-\/point value of zero, the significant and exponent are both zero. For a floating-\/point value that is an infinity or is not a number, the results are undefined.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em gen\+Type} & Floating-\/point scalar or vector types.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/frexp.xml}{\texttt{GLSL frexp man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+3 Common Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_af2b9bdfe77c910ce3ae07c1a386d110e} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_gaf2b9bdfe77c910ce3ae07c1a386d110e}{glm::\+frustum}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{left}{, }\item[{T}]{right}{, }\item[{T}]{bottom}{, }\item[{T}]{top}{, }\item[{T}]{near}{, }\item[{T}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a frustum matrix with default handedness, using the default handedness and default near and far clip planes definition. To change default handedness use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+LEFT\+\_\+\+HANDED. To change default near and far clip planes definition use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE.

\index{intBitsToFloat@{intBitsToFloat}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{intBitsToFloat()}{intBitsToFloat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a5b7b33f0eb5a41f3bf47003bbbdc5128} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} float \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga5b7b33f0eb5a41f3bf47003bbbdc5128}{glm::\+int\+Bits\+To\+Float}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a floating-\/point value corresponding to a signed integer encoding of a floating-\/point value. If an inf or NaN is passed in, it will not signal, and the resulting floating point value is unspecified. Otherwise, the bit-\/level representation is preserved.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

Builds a floating-\/point number from x and the corresponding integral exponent of two in exp, returning:\+ significand \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} exp(2, exponent)

If this product is too large to be represented in the floating-\/point type, the result is undefined.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_ae02d42887fc5570451f880e3c624b9ac} 
template$<$typename gen\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a08b807947b47031d3a511f03f89645ad}{GLM\+\_\+\+CONSTEXPR}} gen\+Type \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gae02d42887fc5570451f880e3c624b9ac}{glm::\+max}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type}]{x}{, }\item[{gen\+Type}]{y}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns y if x \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} y; otherwise, it returns x.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a6b6e0c7ecb4a5b78f929566355bb7416}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!mix@{mix}}
\index{mix@{mix}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mix()}{mix()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a6b6e0c7ecb4a5b78f929566355bb7416} 
template$<$typename gen\+TypeT, typename gen\+TypeU$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a08b807947b47031d3a511f03f89645ad}{GLM\+\_\+\+CONSTEXPR}} gen\+TypeT \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga6b6e0c7ecb4a5b78f929566355bb7416}{glm::\+mix}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+TypeT}]{x}{, }\item[{gen\+TypeT}]{y}{, }\item[{gen\+TypeU}]{a}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

If gen\+TypeU is a floating scalar or vector:\+ Returns x \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} (1.\+0 -\/ a) + y \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} a, i.\+e., the linear blend of x and y using the floating-\/point value a. The value for a is not restricted to the range \+[0, 1]\+.

If gen\+TypeU is a boolean scalar or vector:\+ Selects which vector each returned component comes from. For a component of \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{} that is false, the corresponding component of \textquotesingle{}x\textquotesingle{} is returned. For a component of \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{} that is true, the corresponding component of \textquotesingle{}y\textquotesingle{} is returned. Components of \textquotesingle{}x\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}y\textquotesingle{} that are not selected are allowed to be invalid floating point values and will have no effect on the results. Thus, this provides different functionality than gen\+Type mix(gen\+Type x, gen\+Type y, gen\+Type(a)) where a is a Boolean vector.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/mix.xml}{\texttt{GLSL mix man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+3 Common Functions}}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} gen\+Type \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga85e33f139b8db1b39b590a5713b9e679}{glm::\+modf}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type}]{x}{, }\item[{gen\+Type \&}]{i}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a matrix for an orthographic parallel viewing volume, using left-\/handed coordinates. If GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE is defined, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition) Otherwise, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)

template$<$\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a090a0de2260835bee80e71a702492ed9}{length\+\_\+t}} DA, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a090a0de2260835bee80e71a702492ed9}{length\+\_\+t}} DB, typename T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25}{qualifier}} Q$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1detail_1_1outer_product__trait}{detail::\+outer\+Product\+\_\+trait}}$<$ DA, DB, T, Q $>$\doxymbox{\hyperlink{glad_8h_a890efa53b3d7deeeced6f3a0d6653ed3}{::\+type}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a6f7199140605e146e4f573b72e619187}{glm::\+outer\+Product}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ DA, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{c}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ DB, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{r}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a8c2a0eeee677ca4dafd9e093d9e81062}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!packF2x11\_1x10@{packF2x11\_1x10}}
\index{packF2x11\_1x10@{packF2x11\_1x10}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packF2x11\_1x10()}{packF2x11\_1x10()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a8c2a0eeee677ca4dafd9e093d9e81062} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga8c2a0eeee677ca4dafd9e093d9e81062}{glm::\+pack\+F2x11\+\_\+1x10}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga4320b87e41013b7e875f845f439fc498}{vec3}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, converts the first two components of the normalized floating-\/point value v into 11-\/bit signless floating-\/point values. Then, converts the third component of the normalized floating-\/point value v into a 10-\/bit signless floating-\/point value. Then, the results are packed into the returned 32-\/bit unsigned integer.

The first vector component specifies the 11 least-\/significant bits of the result; the last component specifies the 10 most-\/significant bits.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a0984f9598edc648d59a9643d9a61b121}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!packF3x9\_E1x5@{packF3x9\_E1x5}}
\index{packF3x9\_E1x5@{packF3x9\_E1x5}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a0984f9598edc648d59a9643d9a61b121} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga0984f9598edc648d59a9643d9a61b121}{glm::\+pack\+F3x9\+\_\+\+E1x5}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga4320b87e41013b7e875f845f439fc498}{vec3}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, converts the first two components of the normalized floating-\/point value v into 11-\/bit signless floating-\/point values. Then, converts the third component of the normalized floating-\/point value v into a 10-\/bit signless floating-\/point value. Then, the results are packed into the returned 32-\/bit unsigned integer.

The first vector component specifies the 11 least-\/significant bits of the result; the last component specifies the 10 most-\/significant bits.

pack\+F3x9\+\_\+\+E1x5 allows encoding into RGBE /\+ RGB9\+E5 format

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packHalf()}{packHalf()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a72b41f62169feb06d2c86613b8e1e6bf} 
template$<$\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a090a0de2260835bee80e71a702492ed9}{length\+\_\+t}} L, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25}{qualifier}} Q$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ L, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga6201f5c504a50620708b19bae303c32a}{uint16}}, Q $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga72b41f62169feb06d2c86613b8e1e6bf}{glm::\+pack\+Half}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ L, float, Q $>$ const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns an unsigned integer vector obtained by converting the components of a floating-\/point vector to the 16-\/bit floating-\/point representation found in the Open\+GL Specification. The first vector component specifies the 16 least-\/significant bits of the result; the forth component specifies the 16 most-\/significant bits.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packHalf1x16()}{packHalf1x16()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_aba534b320836a35372e00af5771dd1a2} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga6201f5c504a50620708b19bae303c32a}{uint16}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_gaba534b320836a35372e00af5771dd1a2}{glm::\+pack\+Half1x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns an unsigned integer obtained by converting the components of a floating-\/point scalar to the 16-\/bit floating-\/point representation found in the Open\+GL Specification, and then packing this 16-\/bit value into a 16-\/bit unsigned integer.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_ac29411d6c0f6ed0fe9f0396dfe92e0e8}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!packSnorm1x16@{packSnorm1x16}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packSnorm1x16()}{packSnorm1x16()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_ac29411d6c0f6ed0fe9f0396dfe92e0e8} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga6201f5c504a50620708b19bae303c32a}{uint16}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_gac29411d6c0f6ed0fe9f0396dfe92e0e8}{glm::\+pack\+Snorm1x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, converts the normalized floating-\/point value v into 16-\/bit integer value. Then, the results are packed into the returned 16-\/bit unsigned integer.

The conversion to fixed point is done as follows:\+ pack\+Snorm1x8:\+ round(clamp(s, -\/1, +1) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 32767.\+0)

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packSnorm1x8()}{packSnorm1x8()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a26b6cd7a35c46c4b6a342f3b97b47423} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga536143d82147bb78849bfccffece8bff}{uint8}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga26b6cd7a35c46c4b6a342f3b97b47423}{glm::\+pack\+Snorm1x8}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float}]{s}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, converts the normalized floating-\/point value v into 8-\/bit integer value. Then, the results are packed into the returned 8-\/bit unsigned integer.

The conversion to fixed point is done as follows:\+ pack\+Snorm1x8:\+ round(clamp(s, -\/1, +1) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 127.\+0)

\doxylink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga6201f5c504a50620708b19bae303c32a}{uint16} \doxylink{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a05d08a82923166ec7cd5d0e6154c9953}{pack\+Snorm2x8(vec2 const\& v)} 

\doxylink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32} \doxylink{group__core__func__packing_ga85e8f17627516445026ab7a9c2e3531a}{pack\+Snorm4x8(vec4 const\& v)} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/packSnorm4x8.xml}{\texttt{GLSL pack\+Snorm4x8 man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+4 Floating-\/\+Point Pack and Unpack Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a05d08a82923166ec7cd5d0e6154c9953}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!packSnorm2x8@{packSnorm2x8}}
\index{packSnorm2x8@{packSnorm2x8}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packSnorm2x8()}{packSnorm2x8()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a05d08a82923166ec7cd5d0e6154c9953} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga6201f5c504a50620708b19bae303c32a}{uint16}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga05d08a82923166ec7cd5d0e6154c9953}{glm::\+pack\+Snorm2x8}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga6ebf1ff1f152ff34c800b6997d5f311f}{vec2}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, converts each component of the normalized floating-\/point value v into 8-\/bit integer values. Then, the results are packed into the returned 16-\/bit unsigned integer.

The conversion for component c of v to fixed point is done as follows:\+ pack\+Snorm2x8:\+ round(clamp(c, -\/1, +1) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 127.\+0)

The first component of the vector will be written to the least significant bits of the output; the last component will be written to the most significant bits.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group__gtc__packing}{GLM\+\_\+\+GTC\+\_\+packing} 

\doxylink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga536143d82147bb78849bfccffece8bff}{uint8} pack\+Snorm1x8(float const\& v) 

\doxylink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32} \doxylink{group__core__func__packing_ga85e8f17627516445026ab7a9c2e3531a}{pack\+Snorm4x8(vec4 const\& v)} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/packSnorm4x8.xml}{\texttt{GLSL pack\+Snorm4x8 man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+4 Floating-\/\+Point Pack and Unpack Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a0d4157cec37c0312216a7be1cc92df54}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!packSnorm3x10\_1x2@{packSnorm3x10\_1x2}}
\index{packSnorm3x10\_1x2@{packSnorm3x10\_1x2}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packSnorm3x10\_1x2()}{packSnorm3x10\_1x2()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a0d4157cec37c0312216a7be1cc92df54} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga0d4157cec37c0312216a7be1cc92df54}{glm::\+pack\+Snorm3x10\+\_\+1x2}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga233f0e8f1aecf686e67c5c39316c4da8}{vec4}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, converts the first three components of the normalized floating-\/point value v into 10-\/bit signed integer values. Then, converts the forth component of the normalized floating-\/point value v into 2-\/bit signed integer values. Then, the results are packed into the returned 32-\/bit unsigned integer.

The conversion for component c of v to fixed point is done as follows:\+ pack\+Snorm3x10\+\_\+1x2(xyz):\+ round(clamp(c, -\/1, +1) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 511.\+0) pack\+Snorm3x10\+\_\+1x2(w):\+ round(clamp(c, -\/1, +1) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 1.\+0)

The first vector component specifies the 10 least-\/significant bits of the result; the forth component specifies the 2 most-\/significant bits.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{group__gtc__packing}{GLM\+\_\+\+GTC\+\_\+packing} 

\doxylink{group__core__vector_ga233f0e8f1aecf686e67c5c39316c4da8}{vec4} unpack\+Snorm3x10\+\_\+1x2(uint32 const\& p) 

\doxylink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32} \doxylink{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a2cf2d11b40bd48639110456fd74c2e33}{pack\+Unorm3x10\+\_\+1x2(vec4 const\& v)} 

\doxylink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32} \doxylink{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_af656d8862628f96b20de7a36eaa1fe56}{pack\+U3x10\+\_\+1x2(uvec4 const\& v)} 

\doxylink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32} \doxylink{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a032e18fa5bc5b8f3897104aeb2f1e195}{pack\+I3x10\+\_\+1x2(ivec4 const\& v)}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a9b237d7c66b7a71964e6d1f4dc06539f}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!packSnorm4x16@{packSnorm4x16}}
\index{packSnorm4x16@{packSnorm4x16}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packSnorm4x16()}{packSnorm4x16()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a9b237d7c66b7a71964e6d1f4dc06539f} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_gae3632bf9b37da66233d78930dd06378a}{uint64}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga9b237d7c66b7a71964e6d1f4dc06539f}{glm::\+pack\+Snorm4x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga233f0e8f1aecf686e67c5c39316c4da8}{vec4}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, converts each component of the normalized floating-\/point value v into 16-\/bit integer values. Then, the results are packed into the returned 64-\/bit unsigned integer.

The conversion for component c of v to fixed point is done as follows:\+ pack\+Snorm2x8:\+ round(clamp(c, -\/1, +1) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 32767.\+0)

The first component of the vector will be written to the least significant bits of the output; the last component will be written to the most significant bits.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_af656d8862628f96b20de7a36eaa1fe56} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_gaf656d8862628f96b20de7a36eaa1fe56}{glm::\+pack\+U3x10\+\_\+1x2}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga1f435aa3882ae117565222321adeb3f1}{uvec4}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns an unsigned integer obtained by converting the components of a four-\/component unsigned integer vector to the 10-\/10-\/10-\/2-\/bit unsigned integer representation found in the Open\+GL Specification, and then packing these four values into a 32-\/bit unsigned integer. The first vector component specifies the 10 least-\/significant bits of the result; the forth component specifies the 2 most-\/significant bits.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a833288fc0d4a79f19d0db75a6843bfe6}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!packUnorm2x8@{packUnorm2x8}}
\index{packUnorm2x8@{packUnorm2x8}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packUnorm2x8()}{packUnorm2x8()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a833288fc0d4a79f19d0db75a6843bfe6} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga6201f5c504a50620708b19bae303c32a}{uint16}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga833288fc0d4a79f19d0db75a6843bfe6}{glm::\+pack\+Unorm2x8}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga6ebf1ff1f152ff34c800b6997d5f311f}{vec2}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, converts each component of the normalized floating-\/point value v into 8-\/bit integer values. Then, the results are packed into the returned 16-\/bit unsigned integer.

The conversion for component c of v to fixed point is done as follows:\+ pack\+Unorm2x8:\+ round(clamp(c, 0, +1) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 255.\+0)

The first component of the vector will be written to the least significant bits of the output; the last component will be written to the most significant bits.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a2cf2d11b40bd48639110456fd74c2e33}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!packUnorm3x10\_1x2@{packUnorm3x10\_1x2}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{packUnorm3x10\_1x2()}{packUnorm3x10\_1x2()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a2cf2d11b40bd48639110456fd74c2e33} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga2cf2d11b40bd48639110456fd74c2e33}{glm::\+pack\+Unorm3x10\+\_\+1x2}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga233f0e8f1aecf686e67c5c39316c4da8}{vec4}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, converts the first three components of the normalized floating-\/point value v into 10-\/bit unsigned integer values. Then, converts the forth component of the normalized floating-\/point value v into 2-\/bit signed uninteger values. Then, the results are packed into the returned 32-\/bit unsigned integer.

The conversion for component c of v to fixed point is done as follows:\+ pack\+Unorm3x10\+\_\+1x2(xyz):\+ round(clamp(c, 0, +1) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 1023.\+0) pack\+Unorm3x10\+\_\+1x2(w):\+ round(clamp(c, 0, +1) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 3.\+0)

The first vector component specifies the 10 least-\/significant bits of the result; the forth component specifies the 2 most-\/significant bits.

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_gae3632bf9b37da66233d78930dd06378a}{uint64}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_gac561f06c908b7302537a8ef29fcb409e}{glm::\+pack\+Unorm4x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga233f0e8f1aecf686e67c5c39316c4da8}{vec4}} const \&}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, converts each component of the normalized floating-\/point value v into 16-\/bit integer values. Then, the results are packed into the returned 64-\/bit unsigned integer.

The conversion for component c of v to fixed point is done as follows:\+ pack\+Unorm4x16:\+ round(clamp(c, 0, +1) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 65535.\+0)

The first component of the vector will be written to the least significant bits of the output; the last component will be written to the most significant bits.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a9e13be491fd69a438c8fda440cf0156e}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!perspective@{perspective}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{perspective()}{perspective()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a9e13be491fd69a438c8fda440cf0156e} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_ga9e13be491fd69a438c8fda440cf0156e}{glm::\+perspective}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{fovy}{, }\item[{T}]{aspect}{, }\item[{T}]{near}{, }\item[{T}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a matrix for a symmetric perspective-\/view frustum based on the default handedness and default near and far clip planes definition. To change default handedness use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+LEFT\+\_\+\+HANDED. To change default near and far clip planes definition use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fovy} & Specifies the field of view angle in the y direction. Expressed in radians. \\
\hline
{\em aspect} & Specifies the aspect ratio that determines the field of view in the x direction. The aspect ratio is the ratio of x (width) to y (height). \\
\hline
{\em near} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the near clipping plane (always positive). \\
\hline
{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\em T} & A floating-\/point scalar type \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

Builds a perspective projection matrix based on a field of view and the default handedness and default near and far clip planes definition. To change default handedness use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+LEFT\+\_\+\+HANDED. To change default near and far clip planes definition use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE.

\index{perspectiveFovLH@{perspectiveFovLH}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{perspectiveFovLH()}{perspectiveFovLH()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_af1e5e6d8303f1462e892e0884b66f9fa} 
template$<$typename T$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_gaf1e5e6d8303f1462e892e0884b66f9fa}{glm::\+perspective\+Fov\+LH}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{fov}{, }\item[{T}]{width}{, }\item[{T}]{height}{, }\item[{T}]{near}{, }\item[{T}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Builds a left-\/handed perspective projection matrix based on a field of view. If GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE is defined, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition) Otherwise, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fov} & Expressed in radians. \\
\hline
{\em \doxylink{glad_8h_a09012ea95ebbbe1c032db7c68b54291e}{width}} & Width of the viewport \\

\hline
{\em near} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the near clipping plane (always positive). \\
\hline
{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

template$<$typename T$>$ \\

Creates a matrix for a left-\/handed, symmetric perspective-\/view frustum. If GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE is defined, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition) Otherwise, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fovy} & Specifies the field of view angle, in degrees, in the y direction. Expressed in radians. \\
\hline
{\em aspect} & Specifies the aspect ratio that determines the field of view in the x direction. The aspect ratio is the ratio of x (width) to y (height). \\
\hline
{\em near} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the near clipping plane (always positive). \\
\hline
{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\

\end{DoxyParams}

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25a9d21ccd8b5a009ec7eb7677befc3bf51}{defaultp}} $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__clip__space_ga0786f78f02365fc789c6a4cd809bd441}{glm::\+perspective\+RH}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{T}]{fovy}{, }\item[{T}]{aspect}{, }\item[{T}]{near}{, }\item[{T}]{far}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a matrix for a right-\/handed, symmetric perspective-\/view frustum. If GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE is defined, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of 0 and +1 respectively. (Direct3D clip volume definition) Otherwise, the near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fovy} & Specifies the field of view angle, in degrees, in the y direction. Expressed in radians. \\
\hline
{\em aspect} & Specifies the aspect ratio that determines the field of view in the x direction. The aspect ratio is the ratio of x (width) to y (height). \\
\hline
{\em near} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the near clipping plane (always positive). \\
\hline
{\em far} & Specifies the distance from the viewer to the far clipping plane (always positive).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em T} & A floating-\/point scalar type \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_aa81940d45558cd2ae07fe135e653bcfa}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!round@{round}}
\index{round@{round}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{round()}{round()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_aa81940d45558cd2ae07fe135e653bcfa} 
template$<$\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a090a0de2260835bee80e71a702492ed9}{length\+\_\+t}} L, typename T, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25}{qualifier}} Q$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ L, T, Q $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gaa81940d45558cd2ae07fe135e653bcfa}{glm::\+round}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ L, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a value equal to the nearest integer to x. The fraction 0.\+5 will round in a direction chosen by the implementation, presumably the direction that is fastest. This includes the possibility that round(x) returns the same value as round\+Even(x) for all values of x.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em L} & Integer between 1 and 4 included that qualify the dimension of the vector \\
\hline
{\em T} & Floating-\/point scalar types \\
\hline
{\em Q} & Value from qualifier enum\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a562edf7eca082cc5b7a0aaf180436daf}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!smoothstep@{smoothstep}}
\index{smoothstep@{smoothstep}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{smoothstep()}{smoothstep()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a562edf7eca082cc5b7a0aaf180436daf} 
template$<$typename gen\+Type$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} gen\+Type \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga562edf7eca082cc5b7a0aaf180436daf}{glm::\+smoothstep}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type}]{edge0}{, }\item[{gen\+Type}]{edge1}{, }\item[{gen\+Type}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns 0.\+0 if x \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= edge0 and 1.\+0 if x \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}= edge1 and performs smooth Hermite interpolation between 0 and 1 when edge0 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} x \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} edge1. This is useful in cases where you would want a threshold function with a smooth transition. This is equivalent to:\+ gen\+Type t; t = clamp ((x -\/ edge0) /\+ (edge1 -\/ edge0), 0, 1); return t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} (3 -\/ 2 \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} t); Results are undefined if edge0 \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}= edge1.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em gen\+Type} & Floating-\/point scalar or vector types.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/smoothstep.xml}{\texttt{GLSL smoothstep man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+3 Common Functions}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a774bbb16abffb1644dea6a4cf0f08dac}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!uintBitsToFloat@{uintBitsToFloat}}
\index{uintBitsToFloat@{uintBitsToFloat}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{uintBitsToFloat()}{uintBitsToFloat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a774bbb16abffb1644dea6a4cf0f08dac} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} float \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga774bbb16abffb1644dea6a4cf0f08dac}{glm::\+uint\+Bits\+To\+Float}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}}}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a floating-\/point value corresponding to a unsigned integer encoding of a floating-\/point value. If an inf or NaN is passed in, it will not signal, and the resulting floating point value is unspecified. Otherwise, the bit-\/level representation is preserved.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{http://www.opengl.org/sdk/docs/manglsl/xhtml/uintBitsToFloat.xml}{\texttt{GLSL uint\+Bits\+To\+Float man page}} 

\href{http://www.opengl.org/registry/doc/GLSLangSpec.4.20.8.pdf}{\texttt{GLSL 4.\+20.\+8 specification, section 8.\+3 Common Functions}}

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga4320b87e41013b7e875f845f439fc498}{vec3}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga8b9c7991eb021d95c778bf5c0b2f7824}{glm::\+unpack\+F2x11\+\_\+1x10}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 32-\/bit unsigned integer p into two 11-\/bit signless floating-\/point values and one 10-\/bit signless floating-\/point value . Then, each component is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned three-\/component vector.

The first component of the returned vector will be extracted from the least significant bits of the input; the last component will be extracted from the most significant bits.

First, unpacks a single 32-\/bit unsigned integer p into two 11-\/bit signless floating-\/point values and one 10-\/bit signless floating-\/point value . Then, each component is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned three-\/component vector.

The first component of the returned vector will be extracted from the least significant bits of the input; the last component will be extracted from the most significant bits.

unpack\+F3x9\+\_\+\+E1x5 allows decoding RGBE /\+ RGB9\+E5 data

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} float \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga246f451cebf590726324f7a283e3d65e}{glm::\+unpack\+Snorm1x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga6201f5c504a50620708b19bae303c32a}{uint16}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 16-\/bit unsigned integer p into a single 16-\/bit signed integers. Then, each component is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned scalar.

The conversion for unpacked fixed-\/point value f to floating point is done as follows:\+ unpack\+Snorm1x16:\+ clamp(f /\+ 32767.\+0, -\/1, +1)

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpackSnorm1x8()}{unpackSnorm1x8()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a6f2bebf536fbf7c8b97d4b306bb3354e} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} float \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga6f2bebf536fbf7c8b97d4b306bb3354e}{glm::\+unpack\+Snorm1x8}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga536143d82147bb78849bfccffece8bff}{uint8}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 8-\/bit unsigned integer p into a single 8-\/bit signed integers. Then, the value is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned scalar.

The conversion for unpacked fixed-\/point value f to floating point is done as follows:\+ unpack\+Snorm1x8:\+ clamp(f /\+ 127.\+0, -\/1, +1)

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\doxylink{group__core__vector_ga233f0e8f1aecf686e67c5c39316c4da8}{vec4} \doxylink{group__core__func__packing_ga2db488646d48b7c43d3218954523fe82}{unpack\+Snorm4x8(uint32 p)}

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a27f30f0281b88e152b0895f5e2ead878}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!unpackSnorm2x8@{unpackSnorm2x8}}
\index{unpackSnorm2x8@{unpackSnorm2x8}!glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpackSnorm2x8()}{unpackSnorm2x8()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a27f30f0281b88e152b0895f5e2ead878} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga6ebf1ff1f152ff34c800b6997d5f311f}{vec2}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga27f30f0281b88e152b0895f5e2ead878}{glm::\+unpack\+Snorm2x8}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga6201f5c504a50620708b19bae303c32a}{uint16}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 16-\/bit unsigned integer p into a pair of 8-\/bit signed integers. Then, each component is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned two-\/component vector.

The conversion for unpacked fixed-\/point value f to floating point is done as follows:\+ unpack\+Snorm2x8:\+ clamp(f /\+ 127.\+0, -\/1, +1)

The first component of the returned vector will be extracted from the least significant bits of the input; the last component will be extracted from the most significant bits.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a8b8bb827a3743ca553d8702d3e337101} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga233f0e8f1aecf686e67c5c39316c4da8}{vec4}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga8b8bb827a3743ca553d8702d3e337101}{glm::\+unpack\+Snorm3x10\+\_\+1x2}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 32-\/bit unsigned integer p into four 16-\/bit signed integers. Then, each component is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned four-\/component vector.

The conversion for unpacked fixed-\/point value f to floating point is done as follows:\+ unpack\+Snorm3x10\+\_\+1x2(xyz):\+ clamp(f /\+ 511.\+0, -\/1, +1) unpack\+Snorm3x10\+\_\+1x2(w):\+ clamp(f /\+ 511.\+0, -\/1, +1)

The first component of the returned vector will be extracted from the least significant bits of the input; the last component will be extracted from the most significant bits.

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} float \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga7770e3ade4f4764cc1b2eb42ac4ec188}{glm::\+unpack\+Unorm1x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga6201f5c504a50620708b19bae303c32a}{uint16}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 16-\/bit unsigned integer p into a of 16-\/bit unsigned integers. Then, the value is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned scalar.

The conversion for unpacked fixed-\/point value f to floating point is done as follows:\+ unpack\+Unorm1x16:\+ f /\+ 65535.\+0

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a96ce0c24339ee676e28a027fffd1edf6}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!unpackUnorm2x8@{unpackUnorm2x8}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpackUnorm2x8()}{unpackUnorm2x8()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a96ce0c24339ee676e28a027fffd1edf6} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga6ebf1ff1f152ff34c800b6997d5f311f}{vec2}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_ga96ce0c24339ee676e28a027fffd1edf6}{glm::\+unpack\+Unorm2x8}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga6201f5c504a50620708b19bae303c32a}{uint16}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 16-\/bit unsigned integer p into a pair of 8-\/bit unsigned integers. Then, each component is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned two-\/component vector.

The conversion for unpacked fixed-\/point value f to floating point is done as follows:\+ unpack\+Unorm4x8:\+ f /\+ 255.\+0

The first component of the returned vector will be extracted from the least significant bits of the input; the last component will be extracted from the most significant bits.

\Hypertarget{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_af69ace2b5e9234f8afb4e99c3df1193d}\index{glm::gtc@{glm::gtc}!unpackUnorm3x10\_1x2@{unpackUnorm3x10\_1x2}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unpackUnorm3x10\_1x2()}{unpackUnorm3x10\_1x2()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_af69ace2b5e9234f8afb4e99c3df1193d} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga233f0e8f1aecf686e67c5c39316c4da8}{vec4}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_gaf69ace2b5e9234f8afb4e99c3df1193d}{glm::\+unpack\+Unorm3x10\+\_\+1x2}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_ga22033ef3f73efe1da8e437410adda3be}{uint32}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

First, unpacks a single 32-\/bit unsigned integer p into four 16-\/bit signed integers. Then, each component is converted to a normalized floating-\/point value to generate the returned four-\/component vector.

The conversion for unpacked fixed-\/point value f to floating point is done as follows:\+ unpack\+Snorm3x10\+\_\+1x2(xyz):\+ clamp(f /\+ 1023.\+0, 0, +1) unpack\+Snorm3x10\+\_\+1x2(w):\+ clamp(f /\+ 3.\+0, 0, +1)

The first component of the returned vector will be extracted from the least significant bits of the input; the last component will be extracted from the most significant bits.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_afb2b502bc406031a5618ce930139a9e3} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_a33fdea6f91c5f834105f7415e2a64407}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+QUALIFIER}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__core__vector_ga233f0e8f1aecf686e67c5c39316c4da8}{vec4}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__packing_gafb2b502bc406031a5618ce930139a9e3}{glm::\+unpack\+Unorm4x16}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__uint__sized_gae3632bf9b37da66233d78930dd06378a}{uint64}}}]{p}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unProject()}{unProject()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_aefa35b1dbf52941052a5a3aadc298106} 
template$<$typename T, typename U, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25}{qualifier}} Q$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ 3, T, Q $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__projection_gaefa35b1dbf52941052a5a3aadc298106}{glm::\+un\+Project}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ 3, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{win}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{model}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{proj}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ 4, U, Q $>$ const \&}]{viewport}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Map the specified window coordinates (win.\+x, win.\+y, win.\+z) into object coordinates using default near and far clip planes definition. To change default near and far clip planes definition use GLM\+\_\+\+FORCE\+\_\+\+DEPTH\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+ONE.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em win} & Specify the window coordinates to be mapped. \\
\hline
{\em model} & Specifies the modelview matrix \\
\hline
{\em \doxylink{group__gtx__projection_ga58384b7170801dd513de46f87c7fb00e}{proj}} & Specifies the projection matrix \\
\hline
{\em viewport} & Specifies the viewport \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the computed object coordinates. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em T} & Native type used for the computation. Currently supported:\+ half (not recommended), float or double. \\
\hline
{\em U} & Currently supported:\+ Floating-\/point types and integer types.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\href{https://www.khronos.org/registry/OpenGL-Refpages/gl2.1/xhtml/gluUnProject.xml}{\texttt{glu\+Un\+Project man page}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceglm_1_1gtc_a6214935f32f38e1dc13ba66135eb5784} 
template$<$typename T, typename U, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a36ed105b07c7746804d7fdc7cc90ff25}{qualifier}} Q$>$ \\
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ 3, T, Q $>$ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__matrix__projection_ga6214935f32f38e1dc13ba66135eb5784}{glm::\+un\+Project\+NO}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ 3, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{win}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{model}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1mat}{mat}}$<$ 4, 4, T, Q $>$ const \&}]{proj}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{structglm_1_1vec}{vec}}$<$ 4, U, Q $>$ const \&}]{viewport}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Map the specified window coordinates (win.\+x, win.\+y, win.\+z) into object coordinates. The near and far clip planes correspond to z normalized device coordinates of -\/1 and +1 respectively. (Open\+GL clip volume definition)


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em win} & Specify the window coordinates to be mapped. \\
\hline
{\em model} & Specifies the modelview matrix \\
\hline
{\em \doxylink{group__gtx__projection_ga58384b7170801dd513de46f87c7fb00e}{proj}} & Specifies the projection matrix \\
\hline
{\em viewport} & Specifies the viewport \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the computed object coordinates. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em T} & Native type used for the computation. Currently supported:\+ half (not recommended), float or double. \\
\hline
{\em U} & Currently supported:\+ Floating-\/point types and integer types.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{setup_8hpp_ab2d052de21a70539923e9bcbf6e83a51}{GLM\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+DECL}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespaceglm_a4fd29415871152bfb5abd588334147c8}{uint}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ext__scalar__common_ga9d915647ec33c4110946665f914d3abb}{glm::\+uround}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{gen\+Type const \&}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a value equal to the nearest integer to x. The fraction 0.\+5 will round in a direction chosen by the implementation, presumably the direction that is fastest.
